You can see the Potala Palace from the room. In the morning, you can see the Golden Mountain in the Sunshine of the Potala Palace, and in the evening, you can see the night view of the Potala Palace.

The hotel also provides a 24-hour oxygen concentrator, which is also very good and very friendly to people with altitude sickness. If you must make some suggestions to help the hotel improve, then I will say two words, which is considered to be a bone in the egg. First, the smart lighting in the bathroom area is really useless. It is convenient to sit on the toilet, and you have to shake your body from time to time for the light to turn on again. Do you dare to let the light stay on for a longer time? Second, breakfast starts at 8:30. It may be because I stayed during the Spring Festival, so breakfast started late. But other hotels don‚Äôt have breakfast so late. After all, it is a hotel and needs to be convenient for tourists, so I still hope that this can be improved.

There is also a small refrigerator with Lhasa beer, Coke, Sprite mineral water, green tea, black tea and coffee all available for free. There is also drinking water next to the sink, which is filtered and can be drank directly. There is also a coffee machine.

Cleanliness: The room is very clean, neat and tidy. The stay was very comfortable.

Environment: The hotel is in a very good location. It is very convenient to go out and take a taxi. The environment is also very good.
Service: As soon as you enter the hotel, you can feel the enthusiasm of the hotel staff. The front desk staff are enthusiastic and provide butler-style service. The butler Gu Yue‚Äôs service is very good! kind! Recommend everyone to come to this hotel!
